<userid>115701607717315957103< /userid><username>Paul Vescera<//username><Date>1561318748838< /Date><rate>3</rate>< Text>
Interesting park. On the top of the park there is a BBQ pit and table next to it which is quite unexpected but a good thing. There are picnic like tables there also. If you bring everything you need for a BBQ, then you can have a good experience. If you plan it right and it is a beautiful day outside. It would be an outstanding experience.

Also, it is kid friendly with a small play area and community garden. On one side on top of the park, you can see Parkmerced, San Francisco State University, Stonestown, and Ocean Beach weather permitting.

You can take a nice hike up and down the park. There is a cemented area past the community garden. I think that cemented area could be turned into a either a skate park area or a basketball court.

Other than what I mentioned, it is Ok<//Text>

The only one in fact that didn't have up those misleading double priced gas signs that male you think the has is $0.10 cheaper until you go to the pump and find out that's only if you pay cash or buy a car wash. The pump farthest to the right also very regularly does not accepts cards but when you go inside they say it's you or your card and they've never heard of problems with the machine. Except over the last 3 years it's always happened to me only on that pump through several different cards and I've repeatedly mentioned it to them.< /text>

<Rating>1</Rating><Review>I made the mistake of doing business here last week. I bought a blue 06 Subaru Forester for $5,000 out the door. The salesmen assured me that there were no issues with the car. It looked and drove fine...

When buying, the salesman offered an option of returning the car within two days if I didn't like it. For this privilege, I had to pay $75 up front, and if I brought the car back I would have to pay an additional $175 "restocking" fee. It seemed like a reasonable insurance option, so I opted in.

The next day I took the car to a reputable mechanic for a full inspection. At 133,000 miles one might expect some maintenance, but not like this. Here's what the mechanic found and recommended:

- Left and right cylinder head gaskets leaking engine oil
- Transmission cooler line leaking at radiator
- Transmission fluid, power steering fluid, and brake fluid very dark
- Coolant looks like rust water
- Inside edge of rear tires worn
- Alignment needed
- Front differential and rear differential fluid service due
- Spark plugs (gap at .052 - spec is .039-.049)
- Fuel system cleaning (throttle body coking buildup)
- Struts, coolant hoses, and timing belt all original - past due

For the head gasket repair alone, I was looking at at least $2,000. The mechanic informed me that the previous owner had done a thorough job of cleaning up the spilled oil, so as to hide the fact that the gaskets were leaking. He also said the car did not appear to have been properly maintained ever because many engine components were original and should have been replaced long ago. With the rest of the repairs I was looking at a few more grand, which effectively meant the car was a LEMON.  And even if I wanted to try and salvage the car, some things such as the rust in the coolant system were irreparable.

The mechanic gave me his condolences and suggested that I return the car as soon as possible.

The following day, I returned the car. The salesmen acknowledged the issues and offered to have his mechanic have a look at it (presumably the same mechanic who had ignored and even attempted to conceal these very issues).  I wanted nothing more to do with these people. In the end, I had paid $250 for nothing, not to mention the $100 car inspection, and the time and effort wasted driving an hour back and forth to the dealership three times. Worst of all I still don't have a car.

If for some reason you still choose to go here after reading this review, just a warning: watch out for the blue 06 Subaru Forester. The salesman told me that they would repaint the car, raise the price, and put it back out on the lot for sale.

If I could afford to, I would buy a new car, but I can't, so I buy used. When you're not a mechanic yourself, you have to rely somewhat on the integrity and the decency of the human being selling you the car. Ultimately, I have only myself to blame for getting ripped off. All the same though, I can't comprehend how these people live with themselves.< /Review><pictures>None< /pictures><Response>None<//Response>< Gmap_id>

< text>
I'm a fairly regular patron of Redwing and have been for many years.  It is one of the best dive bars in San Diego that recently (about a year ago) got a bit of a refresh.  It did not lose it's neighbourhood charm with the refresh though, thankfully.  Tracy is my fave bartender!  She remembers everyone even when you haven't been in the bar in a year.  Somehow she even remembers how I love my turkey burger.  That brings me to my point: Redwing turkey burgers are the best burger in San Diego.  That is not an exaggeration either.  I don't eat red meat and I hate veggie burgers well because they're always terrible and the black bean burgers are usually tasteless but when I found the turkey burger at RBG I ate one every day for about 2 weeks.  I've turned hardcore carnivores into a lover of these burgers, too!  I'm sure it is the juices and stuff on the grill from everything else that makes these so delicious but who cares they are...they should be sampled by everyone.  They are always perfectly cooked with the right amount to char and are always super juicy and importantly they are not flattened to death by the chef.
RBG has great drink prices and happy hours plus there is a fantastic jukebox and they have karaoke a couple/few times a week.  If you come in and it's a bit crowded make your way straight through the bar out to the patio where there is a second bar.  The patio bar is usually open Friday through Sunday.< /text>

This is an extremely lovable hole in the wall where some of the best nights of my life have taken place. The atmosphere is fun and welcoming no matter who you are or where your from. Whether your there to sing, dance or just watch, there karaoke nights are an absolute blast; even better, it happens 7 nights a week. It is a tiny space, and after a certain hour it gets super packed; usually with attractive people so the close proximity doesn't bother me. I will say, though that this becomes an issue for any woman that needs to use the restroom. There's only one stall and almost always a line. Other than that tiny setback, if you're looking for a fun place to go out I strongly recommend you give this place a try.< /text>

<userid>106226649654996309969</userid><name>William Williams</name><time>1468978181605<//time><Rating>2<//Rating>< Review>
Redwing is supposed to be the 'gay bar' on North Park but in the last year (2013-2014) it's definitely become overrun with hipsters and straight allies.  Now don't me wrong I'm down with hipsters and allies but damn don't take over queer spaces y'all.

That aside they have a decent sized back patio (smoking section) and AC inside with several TV to watch the game.  They've also started carrying more craft beer and Thursday nights they have great trivia.

This is the place you want to karaoke!!!!  They have a good selection of songs and karaoke almost every night.< /Review>

1522444493033</date>
< Rate>
5< /Rate>
< review>
This is a great neighborhood bar with great food in a great neighborhood. Every bartender I've met so far has got a great personality and are happy to include you in conversations with other new folks and regulars.

I've been twice and had the wings both times and they were excellent also have a dish they called Chick A Rones which are chicken thigh and skin cook very crispy like a chicharron and with a spicy dipping sauce. This is a really excellent dish. I'm looking forward to going back and try new dishes.
I do want to mention that one of the sauces that they offer for dipping or salads or whatever is a cilantro cream sauce which as a lover of cilantro I can highly recommend.

They have lots of lots of different beers on tap as well as the old standby as in bottle and can, I especially like the selection of tall boys  they offer, especially if you like to drink old school!!</review>
